I developed a new workshop concept:
â€œProduct Management Essentials: Engineering Insights & Smart AI Tools for the Modern PMâ€

Workshop Overview:
This workshop is designed to equip young product managers with a solid foundation in engineering principles and a strategic approach to the product lifecycle. By combining engineering insights with selective AI applications, participants will gain a well-rounded toolkit to manage product development end-to-end, drive effective decision-making, and align with technical teams.

Target Audience:
Ideal for early-career product managers and aspiring PMs who seek to strengthen their technical knowledge, understand the product lifecycle, and learn to use AI tools that complement their strategic goals.

Key Learning Objectives:
Participants will gain skills to:

	1.	Navigate the Product Lifecycle: Understand the full lifecycle from ideation to launch and retirement, learning best practices for each phase and critical metrics to measure success.
	2.	Enhance Collaboration with Engineering: Gain insights into technical basics, enabling better collaboration with engineering teams and smoother product execution.
	3.	Apply AI as a Strategic Tool: Leverage AI selectively to support data-driven decision-making, customer insights, and competitive analysis, enhancing PM efficiency without overwhelming the focus on core PM and engineering knowledge.
	4.	Streamline Development Processes: Learn how to use AI and automation where valuable, such as in testing and monitoring, to save time and maintain quality across the product lifecycle.
	5.	Ensure Product Integrity with Ethical AI Use: Recognize ethical considerations and potential risks of AI usage, ensuring responsible integration that maintains user trust.
